\DoxyCodeLine{00965\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ approximation\ of\ 1/b.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00966\ \ \ restep\ =\ vrecps\_f32(b,\ inv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00967\ \ \ inv\ =\ vmul\_f32(restep,\ inv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00968\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00969\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Finally,\ multiply\ a\ by\ 1/b\ and\ get\ the\ wanted\ result\ of\ the\ division.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00970\ \ \ div\ =\ vmul\_f32(a,\ inv);}
\DoxyCodeLine{00971\ }
